{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36}{op\+::\+Thread\+Manager\+Mode}} \+: unsigned char\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_thread_manager}{Thread\+Manager}} synchronization mode. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{열거형 멤버}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Asynchronous@{Asynchronous}!op@{op}}\index{op@{op}!Asynchronous@{Asynchronous}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36a288aae25bc408055f50c21c991903a44}\label{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36a288aae25bc408055f50c21c991903a44}} 
Asynchronous&First and last queues of \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_thread_manager}{Thread\+Manager}} will be given to the user, so he must push elements to the first queue and retrieve them from the last one after being processed. Recommended for prototyping environments (easier to test but more error-\/prone and potentially slower in performance). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AsynchronousIn@{AsynchronousIn}!op@{op}}\index{op@{op}!AsynchronousIn@{AsynchronousIn}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36a435b3ab344c03bfc0e4530a2e75f5e44}\label{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36a435b3ab344c03bfc0e4530a2e75f5e44}} 
Asynchronous\+In&Similar to Asynchronous, but only the input (first) queue is given to the user. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{AsynchronousOut@{AsynchronousOut}!op@{op}}\index{op@{op}!AsynchronousOut@{AsynchronousOut}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36ac68f8680ccf3a65dfcfc63356112c9f9}\label{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36ac68f8680ccf3a65dfcfc63356112c9f9}} 
Asynchronous\+Out&Similar to Asynchronous, but only the output (last) queue is given to the user. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Synchronous@{Synchronous}!op@{op}}\index{op@{op}!Synchronous@{Synchronous}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36a2fe4167817733fec8e6ba1afddf78f1b}\label{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36a2fe4167817733fec8e6ba1afddf78f1b}} 
Synchronous&Everything will run inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_thread_manager}{Thread\+Manager}}. Recommended for production environments (more difficult to set up but faster in performance and less error-\/prone). \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}

\index{op@{op}!configureThreadManager@{configureThreadManager}}
\index{configureThreadManager@{configureThreadManager}!op@{op}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{configureThreadManager()}{configureThreadManager()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T\+Datum , typename T\+Datums  = std\+::vector$<$std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$\+T\+Datum$>$$>$, typename T\+Datums\+SP  = std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$\+T\+Datums$>$, typename T\+Worker  = std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$\+Worker$<$\+T\+Datums\+S\+P$>$$>$$>$ \\
void op\+::configure\+Thread\+Manager (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_thread_manager}{Thread\+Manager}}$<$ T\+Datums\+SP $>$ \&}]{thread\+Manager,  }\item[{const bool}]{multi\+Thread\+Enabled,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceop_a3593e2d53bec533f0048ef3973eebd36}{Thread\+Manager\+Mode}}}]{thread\+Manager\+Mode,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structop_1_1_wrapper_struct_pose}{Wrapper\+Struct\+Pose}} \&}]{wrapper\+Struct\+Pose,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structop_1_1_wrapper_struct_face}{Wrapper\+Struct\+Face}} \&}]{wrapper\+Struct\+Face,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structop_1_1_wrapper_struct_hand}{Wrapper\+Struct\+Hand}} \&}]{wrapper\+Struct\+Hand,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structop_1_1_wrapper_struct_extra}{Wrapper\+Struct\+Extra}} \&}]{wrapper\+Struct\+Extra,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structop_1_1_wrapper_struct_input}{Wrapper\+Struct\+Input}} \&}]{wrapper\+Struct\+Input,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structop_1_1_wrapper_struct_output}{Wrapper\+Struct\+Output}} \&}]{wrapper\+Struct\+Output,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structop_1_1_wrapper_struct_gui}{Wrapper\+Struct\+Gui}} \&}]{wrapper\+Struct\+Gui,  }\item[{const std\+::array$<$ std\+::vector$<$ T\+Worker $>$, int(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceop_a970a2a768a2ace81605b1558c9fdec18a6f6cb72d544962fa333e2e34ce64f719}{Worker\+Type\+::\+Size}})$>$ \&}]{user\+Ws,  }\item[{const std\+::array$<$ bool, int(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceop_a970a2a768a2ace81605b1558c9fdec18a6f6cb72d544962fa333e2e34ce64f719}{Worker\+Type\+::\+Size}})$>$ \&}]{user\+Ws\+On\+New\+Thread }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_thread_manager}{Thread\+Manager}} from T\+Workers (private internal function). After any configure() has been called, the T\+Workers are initialized. This function resets the \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_thread_manager}{Thread\+Manager}} and adds them. Common code for start() and exec(). 

wrapper\+Auxiliary.\+hpp 파일의 87 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceop_a5f092bd36c716a894cb035e1ead2aca3}\label{namespaceop_a5f092bd36c716a894cb035e1ead2aca3}} 
\index{op@{op}!error@{error}}
\index{error@{error}!op@{op}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{error()}{error()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{macros_8hpp_a4ba443bb7a0e5dbe8054a9ac37a5e000}{O\+P\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} void op\+::error (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{message,  }\item[{const int}]{line = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{function = {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\char`\"{}},  }\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{file = {\ttfamily \char`\"{}\char`\"{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Differences between different kind of errrors\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceop_a5f092bd36c716a894cb035e1ead2aca3}{error()}} is a normal error in the code.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceop_a61af88aac41ef77ab4e8816023fe32f0}{error\+Worker()}} is an error that occurred on a thread. Therefore, the machine will stop the threads, go back to the main thread, and then throw the error.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceop_a825f15fdf9dc9cb7473c20f970f15b60}{error\+Destructor()}} is an error that occurred on a destructor. Exception on destructors provokes core dumped, so we simply output an error message via std\+::cerr. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceop_a42d364d9fbd1a719341bd7187d97cf18}\label{namespaceop_a42d364d9fbd1a719341bd7187d97cf18}} 
\index{op@{op}!error@{error}}
\index{error@{error}!op@{op}}

\index{formatAsDirectory@{formatAsDirectory}!op@{op}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{formatAsDirectory()}{formatAsDirectory()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{macros_8hpp_a4ba443bb7a0e5dbe8054a9ac37a5e000}{O\+P\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} std\+::string op\+::format\+As\+Directory (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{directory\+Path\+String }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This function makes sure that the directory\+Path\+String is properly formatted. I.\+e., it changes all \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}\textquotesingle{} by \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{}, and it makes sure that the string finishes with \textquotesingle{}/\textquotesingle{}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em directory\+Path\+String} & std\+::string with the directory path to be formatted. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
std\+::string with the formatted directory path. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
이 함수를 호출하는 함수들에 대한 그래프입니다.\+:\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]

\index{op@{op}!getKeypointsPerson@{getKeypointsPerson}}
\index{getKeypointsPerson@{getKeypointsPerson}!op@{op}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getKeypointsPerson()}{getKeypointsPerson()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T $>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_array}{Array}}$<$T$>$ op\+::get\+Keypoints\+Person (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_array}{Array}}$<$ T $>$ \&}]{keypoints,  }\item[{const int}]{person,  }\item[{const bool}]{no\+Copy = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates and Array$<$\+T$>$ with a specific person. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em keypoints} & Array$<$\+T$>$ with the original data array to slice. \\
\hline
{\em person} & indicates the index of the array to extract. \\
\hline
{\em no\+Copy} & indicates whether to perform a copy. Copy will never go to undefined behavior, however, if no\+Copy == true, then\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item It is faster, as no data copy is involved, but...
\item If the \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_array}{Array}} keypoints goes out of scope, then the resulting \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_array}{Array}} will provoke an undefined behavior.
\item If the returned \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_array}{Array}} is modified, the information in the \mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_array}{Array}} keypoints will also be. 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
Array$<$\+T$>$ with the same dimension than keypoints expect the first dimension being 1. E.\+g., if keypoints is \{p,k,m\}, the resulting Array$<$\+T$>$ is \{1,k,m\}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{op@{op}!mergeVectors@{mergeVectors}}
\index{mergeVectors@{mergeVectors}!op@{op}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mergeVectors()}{mergeVectors()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T $>$ \\
std\+::vector$<$T$>$ op\+::merge\+Vectors (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ T $>$ \&}]{vectorA,  }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ T $>$ \&}]{vectorB }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

std\+::vector$<$\+T$>$ concatenator. Auxiliary function that concatenate std\+::vectors of any class type T. It assumes basic copy (ideal for smart pointers, pointers, etc.), so note that the copy still shares the same internal data. It will not work for element that cannot be copied. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em vectorA} & First std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$\+T$>$ element to be concatenated. \\
\hline
{\em vectorB} & Second std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$\+T$>$ element to be concatenated. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{반환값}
Concatenated std\+::vector$<$\+T$>$ of both vectorA and vectorB. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classop_1_1_thread}{Thread}} ID increase (private internal function). If multi-\/threading mode, it increases the thread ID. If single-\/threading mode (for debugging), it does not modify it. Note that m\+Thread\+Id must be re-\/initialized to 0 before starting a new Wrapper(\+T) configuration. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}

3D triangulation given known camera parameter matrices and based on linear D\+LT algorithm. The returned cv\+::\+Mat is a 4x1 matrix, where the last coordinate is 1. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceop_a8b4504cce89493c23233954f078f4779}\label{namespaceop_a8b4504cce89493c23233954f078f4779}}

\index{triangulateWithOptimization@{triangulateWithOptimization}!op@{op}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{triangulateWithOptimization()}{triangulateWithOptimization()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{macros_8hpp_a4ba443bb7a0e5dbe8054a9ac37a5e000}{O\+P\+\_\+\+A\+PI}} double op\+::triangulate\+With\+Optimization (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{cv\+::\+Mat \&}]{reconstructed\+Point,  }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ cv\+::\+Mat $>$ \&}]{camera\+Matrices,  }\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ cv\+::\+Point2d $>$ \&}]{points\+On\+Each\+Camera,  }\item[{const double}]{reprojection\+Max\+Acceptable }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

3D triangulation given known camera parameter matrices and based on linear D\+LT algorithm with additional L\+MA non-\/linear refinement. The returned cv\+::\+Mat is a 4x1 matrix, where the last coordinate is 1. Note\+: If Ceres is not enabled, the L\+MA refinement is skipped and this function is equivalent to \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceop_ae541aa57d03a703ab8b1da231e06a9bd}{triangulate()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceop_af548fe1a2ad2b392a25afe9b0b87b8dd}\label{namespaceop_af548fe1a2ad2b392a25afe9b0b87b8dd}}
